## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Agentic Correctness: Implement Kubernetes Custom Resource Client

## Your Task

Write a Go file `crd_client.go` that implements a typed client for a custom resource `Widget` (group `example.com`, version `v1`). Your implementation must follow the patterns established in the Kubernetes client-go codebase: 1. Embed or use the `rest.Interface` client from `k8s.io/client-go/rest`. 2. Implement `Create`, `Get`, `List`, and `Delete` methods following the same parameter conventions as `k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/typed/` clients. 3. Use proper `context.Context` propagation. Write your implementation to `/workspace/crd_client.go`. Also write `/workspace/answer.json` listing the client-go source files you referenced.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?
- **Keyword presence**: Are required terms present in your explanation?

Perfect! I've successfully created the implementation. Let me verify the solution is complete:

## Summary

I've created a typed Kubernetes custom resource client for a `Widget` resource in the `example.com` API group v1. The implementation includes:

### `/workspace/crd_client.go`
- **Widget and WidgetList types**: Custom resource definitions with proper Kubernetes object structure
- **WidgetInterface**: Defines the contract with `Create`, `Get`, `List`, and `Delete` methods
- **WidgetsGetter**: Interface for accessing widget clients by namespace
- **widgets struct**: Concrete implementation that:
  - Embeds `rest.Interface` from `k8s.io/client-go/rest`
  - Uses fluent builder pattern for REST requests (`.Post().Namespace().Resource().Name().Do().Into()`)
  - Properly propagates `context.Context` in all methods
- **ExampleV1Client**: Group-level client that manages the REST client and parameter codec
- **Factory functions**: `NewForConfig`, `NewForConfigAndClient`, `NewForConfigOrDie`, and `New`
- **Configuration**: `setConfigDefaults` sets the GroupVersion to `example.com/v1` and APIPath to `/apis`

### Key Implementation Details:
1. **Context Propagation**: All CRUD methods accept `context.Context` as the first parameter for proper cancellation/timeout handling
2. **REST Client Usage**: Uses the standard Kubernetes request builder pattern (Post/Get/Delete chains)
3. **Parameter Codec**: Properly handles versioned parameters for API options
4. **Resource Methods**: All methods follow the same parameter conventions as `k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/typed/` clients

### `/workspace/answer.json`
Documents the source files referenced from the client-go codebase:
- Core pattern files: `configmap.go`, `namespace.go`, `core_client.go`
- Implementation details: `gentype/type.go

	"k8s.io/client-go/rest"

// Widget is a custom resource representing a widget in the example.com API group.
// This is a simplified example; in a real implementation, Widget would be defined in a separate API package.
type Widget struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Spec              WidgetSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetSpec is the specification for a Widget.
type WidgetSpec struct {
	// Name is the display name of the widget
	Name string `json:"name,omitempty"`
	// Color is the color of the widget
	Color string `json:"color,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetList is a list of Widget objects.
type WidgetList struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Items           []Widget `json:"items"`
}

// DeepCopyObject implements runtime.Object for Widget.
func (w *Widget) DeepCopyObject() runtime.Object {
	if w == nil {
		return nil
	}
	return &Widget{
		TypeMeta:   w.TypeMeta,
		ObjectMeta: *w.ObjectMeta.DeepCopy(),
		Spec:       w.Spec,
	}
}

// Create takes the representation of a widget and creates it. Returns the server's representation of the widget, and an error, if there is any.
func (c *widgets) Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := c.client.Post().
		Namespace(c.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		VersionedParams(&opts, runtime.NewParameterCodec(runtime.NewScheme())).
		Body(widget).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// Get takes name of the widget, and returns the corresponding widget object, and an error if there is any.
func (c *widgets) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error) {

		Namespace(c.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		Name(name).
		VersionedParams(&opts, runtime.NewParameterCodec(runtime.NewScheme())).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

7. EDIT /workspace/crd_client.go
Before
// NewForConfigAndClient creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config and http client.
// Note the http client provided takes precedence over the configured transport values.
func NewForConfigAndClient(c *rest.Config, h *http.Client) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {
	config := *c
	if err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	client, err := rest.RESTClientForConfigAndClient(&config, h)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return &ExampleV1Client{client}, nil
}
After
// NewForConfigAndClient creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config and http client.
// Note the http client provided takes precedence over the configured transport values.
func NewForConfigAndClient(c *rest.Config, h *http.Client) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {
	config := *c
	if err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	client, err := rest.RESTClientForConfigAndClient(&config, h)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return &ExampleV1Client{
		restClient:     client,
		parameterCodec: runtime.NewParameterCodec(runtime.NewScheme()),
	}, nil
}

9. EDIT /workspace/crd_client.go
Before
func setConfigDefaults(config *rest.Config) error {
	config.GroupVersion = &metav1.GroupVersion{Group: "example.com", Version: "v1"}
	config.APIPath = "/apis"
	config.NegotiatedSerializer = rest.CodecFactoryForGeneratedClient(
		runtime.NewScheme(),
		runtime.NewCodecFactory(runtime.NewScheme()).WithoutConversion(),
	).WithoutConversion()

	if config.UserAgent == "" {
		config.UserAgent = rest.DefaultKubernetesUserAgent()
	}

	return nil
}
After
func setConfigDefaults(config *rest.Config) error {
	gv := schema.GroupVersion{Group: "example.com", Version: "v1"}
	config.GroupVersion = &gv
	config.APIPath = "/apis"

	// Create a minimal scheme for the Widget type
	scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
	config.NegotiatedSerializer = serializer.NewCodecFactory(scheme).WithoutConversion()

	if config.UserAgent == "" {
		config.UserAgent = rest.DefaultKubernetesUserAgent()
	}

	return nil
}
